 - input IANS The dramatic references to human life are deeply identified in the writings of Krishna Baldev Vaid

 uskaa bachapan, bimal urf jaayen to jaayen kahaan, tasareen, doosraa na koi, dard laa dawa, guzara hua zamana, kaala kolaj, nar nari, maaya lok, ek naukaraani kii diary jaise upanyaason se unhone hindi sahitya main apni ek alag hi pahchaan banaai
 In the story collections he wrote; The middle door, my enemy, from the other shore, missing, his statements, my favorite stories, he and I, silence, alas, representative stories, leela, famous stories, fathers shadows, ten representative stories, Bodhisattva's wife, raffish wives Island of the whole, stories of mine, night walk etc
 are important
 unka likhaa upanyaas 'ek naukaraani kii diary' shahari jivan ke us upekshit tabake par kendrit he jisaki samasyaon par ham samvedansheel tareeke se kabhi baat nahin karte magar jiske bina hamaara kaam bhi nahin chal paata
